{\footnotesize\ttfamily void v8\+::internal\+::compiler\+::\+Raw\+Machine\+Assembler\+::\+Pop\+And\+Return (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1internal_1_1compiler_1_1Node}{Node}} $\ast$}]{pop,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1internal_1_1compiler_1_1Node}{Node}} $\ast$}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Definition at line 632 of file raw-\/machine-\/assembler.\+cc.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{632                                                              \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{633   \textcolor{comment}{// PopAndReturn is supposed to be used ONLY in CSA/Torque builtins for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{634   \textcolor{comment}{// dropping ALL JS arguments that are currently located on the stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{635   \textcolor{comment}{// The check below ensures that there are no directly accessible stack}}
\DoxyCodeLine{636   \textcolor{comment}{// parameters from current builtin, which implies that the builtin with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{637   \textcolor{comment}{// JS calling convention (TFJ) was created with kDontAdaptArgumentsSentinel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{638   \textcolor{comment}{// This simplifies semantics of this instruction because in case of presence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{639   \textcolor{comment}{// of directly accessible stack parameters it's impossible to distinguish}}
\DoxyCodeLine{640   \textcolor{comment}{// the following cases:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{641   \textcolor{comment}{// 1) stack parameter is included in JS arguments (and therefore it will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{642   \textcolor{comment}{//    dropped as a part of 'pop' number of arguments),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{643   \textcolor{comment}{// 2) stack parameter is NOT included in JS arguments (and therefore it should}}
\DoxyCodeLine{644   \textcolor{comment}{//    be dropped in ADDITION to the 'pop' number of arguments).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{645   \textcolor{comment}{// Additionally, in order to simplify assembly code, PopAndReturn is also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{646   \textcolor{comment}{// not allowed in builtins with stub linkage and parameters on stack.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{647   \mbox{\hyperlink{src_2base_2logging_8h_aca32614b4d2aea7dd9abdeb222bf02f3}{CHECK\_EQ}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1internal_1_1compiler_1_1RawMachineAssembler_aa32ae3c954df4facdc8e402cbf598679}{call\_descriptor}}()-\/>ParameterSlotCount(), 0);}
